**GT expression:**
`0.845*(−1 + P/5.115)*(1 − P/34.44)*P + 0.845*(1 − exp(−0.0969*P))*P`

Let me expand this:

**First term:** `0.845*(P/5.115 − 1)*(1 − P/34.44)*P`

Expanding `(P/5.115 − 1)*(1 − P/34.44)`:
= P/5.115 − P²/(5.115×34.44) − 1 + P/34.44
= −P²/176.16 + P(1/5.115 + 1/34.44) − 1
= −P²/176.16 + P(0.1955 + 0.02904) − 1
= −P²/176.16 + 0.2245P − 1

Multiply by 0.845*P:
= −0.845P³/176.16 + 0.845×0.2245P² − 0.845P
= −0.004797P³ + 0.1897P² − 0.845P

**Second term:** `0.845*(1 − exp(−0.0969P))*P`
= 0.845P − 0.845P·exp(−0.0969P)

**Total GT:**
= −0.004797P³ + 0.1897P² − 0.845P + 0.845P − 0.845P·exp(−0.0969P)
= −0.004797P³ + 0.1897P² − 0.845P·exp(−0.0969P)

So GT = **c0·P³ + c1·P² + c2·P·exp(c3·P)** where c0 ≈ −0.0048, c1 ≈ 0.19, c2 ≈ −0.845, c3 ≈ −0.0969.

**Candidate 25:** `P**3*c0 + P**2*c1 + P*c2`
This has P³ + P² + P but no exponential term. Not a match.

**Candidate 26:** `P**3*c0 + P**2*c1 + P*c2*exp(P*c3) + P*c4 + P*c5 + c6*t*exp(c7*t)`
= P³·c0 + P²·c1 + P·c2·exp(P·c3) + P·(c4+c5) + c6·t·exp(c7·t)

## Ground Truth Analysis

The GT is:
```
0.845*(P/5.115 - 1)*(1 - P/34.44)*P + 0.845*(1 - exp(-0.0969*P))*P
```

Let me expand this:
- First term: `0.845*(P/5.115 - 1)*(1 - P/34.44)*P`
  - `= 0.845*(P²/5.115 - P²/(5.115*34.44) - P + P/34.44)*P`... let me be more careful.
  - `(P/5.115 - 1)(1 - P/34.44) = P/5.115 - P²/(5.115*34.44) - 1 + P/34.44`
  - Multiply by P: `P²/5.115 - P³/(5.115*34.44) - P + P²/34.44`
  - Multiply by 0.845: `0.845*P²/5.115 - 0.845*P³/(5.115*34.44) - 0.845*P + 0.845*P²/34.44`

- Second term: `0.845*(1 - exp(-0.0969*P))*P = 0.845*P - 0.845*P*exp(-0.0969*P)`

Combining:
- P³ term: `-0.845/(5.115*34.44) * P³ ≈ -0.004797*P³`
- P² term: `0.845/5.115 + 0.845/34.44 ≈ 0.16520 + 0.02453 ≈ 0.18973*P²`
- P term: `-0.845*P + 0.845*P = 0` (the linear P terms cancel!)
- Exponential term: `-0.845*P*exp(-0.0969*P)`

So GT = **a*P³ + b*P² + c*P*exp(d*P)** where a < 0, b > 0, d < 0.

This is the key structure: **P³ + P² + P*exp(negative*P)**

Now let me check each candidate:

### Candidate 1: P³c0 + P²c1 + P²c2 + P²c3 + Pc4 + Pc5 + c6
= P³c0 + P²(c1+c2+c3) + P(c4+c5) + c6
This is a cubic polynomial. GT has P*exp(d*P) which cannot be represented by a polynomial.
**Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 2: P²c0 + Pc1 + Pc2*exp(c3*t) + c4 + c5*exp(P²c6 + Pc7)
Has t-dependence (can set c2=0 to remove), then: P²c0 + Pc1 + c4 + c5*exp(P²c6 + Pc7)
GT needs P³ term and P*exp(P) term. This has exp(P²c6 + Pc7) which is not P*exp(P). Missing P³.
**Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 3: P³c0 + P²c1 + Pc2*log(Pc3+1) + c4 + c5*exp(P²c6 + Pc7)
Has P³, P², P*log(P+1), and exp(P²+P). GT needs P*exp(P). log and exp(P²) are wrong basis functions.
**Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 4: P³c0 + P²(c1+c2+c3+c4) + P(c5+c6+c7) + c8
Cubic polynomial. Missing P*exp(P).
**Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 7: P²c0*exp(c1*t) + Pc2*exp(c1*t) + Pc3/(P+c4) + Pc5*exp(Pc6) + c7 + c8*exp(c9*t)

Has P*exp(Pc6) ✓, but needs P³. Pc3/(P+c4) = c3*P²/(P+c4) which isn't P³. P²c0 + Pc3/(P+c4) with common denominator = (P²c0(P+c4) + Pc3)/(P+c4) = (c0P³ + c0c4P² + c3P)/(P+c4). This is a rational function, not a polynomial P³.

= P³c0 + P²c1 + P*a + P*c2*exp(Pc3)

GT = a*P³ + b*P² + c*P*exp(d*P) (with the linear P terms canceling to 0).

This candidate has: P³c0 + P²c1 + P*(c4+c5) + Pc2*exp(Pc3)

Set c4+c5 = 0, then: P³c0 + P²c1 + Pc2*exp(Pc3)

This matches the GT structure! GT = aP³ + bP² + cP*exp(dP) with a≈-0.004797, b≈0.18973, c≈-0.845, d≈-0.0969.

Set c0 = -0.004797, c1 = 0.18973, c2 = -0.845, c3 = -0.0969, c4+c5 = 0.

**Candidate 26 verdict: [MATCH]**
